 India Post, the world's largest postal network, is creating a separate entity for managing bank services which will help it connect its atms with the ATM network of public sector banks
 india post ko pichley saal bhugtan bank ke parichaalan ke liye license mila tha or vah parichaalan shuru karne kii disha main zyada aage nahin bad paaya he
 "we wanted to connect the atms of post offices with other banks," said a finance ministry official
 arabiai ne kaha ki ham isaki manjuuri tabhi de sakate hai jabaki dak ghar ek alag bank ikai banaaen kyonki arabiai ke adhikaar kshetra main sirf bank hai
 The postal department has adopted a positive attitude and created a separate entity
 " is ikai kaa mukhyalay bengalooru hoga
 After contacting the ATM network, people will have the facility to transfer money from their post office account to a bank account
 iske alaava dak ghar ke atm kaa upyog bank khaaton se dhan nikaale jane ke liye bhi kiya ja sakegaa
 The official said that this unit has been created to bring the post bank license into operation and eventually it will be merged with the post bank
 dak vibhaag ke desh bhar main 28,000 vibhageeya dak ghar or 1
 There are post offices in 5 million rural areas
 dak vibhaag gramin dak gharon main atm or chote atm laga rahaa he taaki vittiya samavesh ke liye vistrut network kaa phayda uthaaya ja sake
 "the RBI said that a separate unit of the Department of Posts has been constituted for banking regulation," the official said
 arabiai atm ko samgr network se jodne ke sambandh main vikalp par vichaar kar rahaa he
 "this will help in moving towards a less cash economy," he said
 dak vibhaag kii aise dur-daraaj ilaakon main bhi shakhaaen hai jahaan bank mitra kii pahunch nahin ho sakati
 The interconnecting of atms will allow the Department of Posts to take advantage of access to far flung areas
 '' post bank kaa aupchaarik dhaancha kareeb dedh saal main aakaar legaa
 Therefore, the government wants the post bank to start its operations through the post office ATM
